######################################################
# Idea Variation 2 Ideagroups Added on country formation/revolts

iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revolt_country = {

iv2_scripted_effect_ig_form_country = {
	add_country_modifier = { 
		modifier = iv2_country_formation_modifier
		years = 30 
		size = {
			value = 1
			
			if = {
				limit = { current_year > 1400	}
				add = {
					value = 1
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { current_year > 1500	}
				add = {
					value = 1
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { current_year > 1600	}
				add = {
					value = 1
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { current_year > 1700	}
				add = {
					value = 1
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { current_year > 1800	}
				add = {
					value = 2
				}
			}
		} 
	}
}
